The 14th New Jersey Volunteer Infantry Monument was established on 11 July 1907 and is located in the district of the Monocacy National Battlefield in Frederick County, Maryland, US. The monument is owned by the National Park Service. The nearest city to the battlefield is Frederick, Maryland.

The 14th New Jersey Volunteer Infantry Monument is found in the Monocacy National Battlefield, Frederick County, Maryland. Located near to the city of Frederick, the monument was established on 11th July 1907, is owned by the National Park Service and belongs to the category of Historic districts in the United States.
